 To fully enjoy high levels of physical and mental health, tell people about their right to good health and healthy lifestyle

 To make people aware of physical and mental illnesses and make it available through yoga
 3
 Make the habit of meditation in people through yoga

 To attract the attention of people all over the world towards the overall benefits of yoga

 Reducing the rate of health-challenging diseases worldwide

 Bringing communities closer to health by taking a day off from a hectic routine

 Spreading growth, development and peace throughout the world

 Helping people in their bad situation by providing relief from stress through yoga

 To strengthen global coordination among people through yoga
